select s.objid, s.ra, s.dec, s.u, s.g, s.err_g, s.r,s.err_r, s.i,s.err_i, s.z, s.g-s.r as g_minus_r, s.type into mydb.MyTable1 from star s, dbo.fGetNearbyObjEq(#,#,#) n  where   s.objid = n.objid and   s.type=# and   s.err_r<#   and s.r<#
select s.objid, s.ra, s.dec, s.u, s.g, s.err_g, s.r,s.err_r, s.i,s.err_i, s.z, s.g-s.r as g_minus_r, s.type into mydb.MyTable from star s, dbo.fGetNearbyObjEq(#,#,#) n  where   s.objid = n.objid and   s.type=# and   s.err_r<#   and s.r<#
SELECT TOP #  p.objid,p.ra,p.dec,p.u,p.g,p.r,p.i,p.z,s.z FROM PhotoObj AS p  JOIN SpecObj AS s ON s.bestobjid = p.objid  AND s.z AS redshift WHERE   p.ra BETWEEN # AND #  AND p.dec BETWEEN # AND #  AND s.z<#
